Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Real World and the World of God's Will
If there are people here who are seeing me for the first time, please raise your hand. 
Put it down. You must have been curious about what kind of person the teacher is when you came here.
Daegu, which has faced much persecution from the Unification Church
As you know, Daegu is a city that can be considered the center of Christianity in our Korea. When you think of 'Daegu,' you always think of 'big hill.' In other words, the character for 'big (大)' and the character for 'hill (丘)' come to mind. Also, when it comes to fish, we say 'myeongtae' and 'daegu,' right? (laughter)
When we held the 'Day of Hope Grand Festival,' a big fight started with the established churches in Daegu. So, for the teacher, Daegu is always an unforgettable city, the center of persecution. Do you feel good? "Not good." What kind of elder are you? You are the mother-in-law of the pastor of the First Church, what kind of elder are you? "Elder Lim." Elder Lim! Do your sons-in-law still oppose you? "……" They don’t oppose you? "Yes."
As I entered Daegu today, I thought about…. How many years ago would it be? It was in 1954, so it was over 20 years ago when the teacher lived here on October 28, 1978 (Saturday), Daegu Church.
* This speech was given during a tour of the Gyeongbuk district.
8   The Real World and the World of God's Will
I faced so much opposition that I moved more than a dozen times in a month. Do you understand? When someone named Moon came to Daegu, the established churches immediately notified each other and ordered their congregants to 'drive that strange person away.' This reminds me of all the times I had to move.
Compared to that time, I feel that things have changed a lot now. Back then, I was the subject of attention from the police authorities, and wherever I went, there was a label that I was a strange person, but now things have changed a lot. Just as our human world, our living conditions, our environment, our public sentiment, and our history are changing.
The people of Gyeongbuk must unite and advance centered on Daegu
For nearly three years, for about two and a half years, you have been hoping for the teacher's return, but I was late in returning because I had responsibilities abroad. I apologize for that.
Now that I am here in Daegu, I would like to give good words to the Daegu members and praise them so that they can say, 'Our teacher is the best.' However, I feel that I cannot say such things. As I sat quietly and prayed, I thought about 'Daegu' as the center of Gyeongsangbuk-do and a central city in the current government. I do not know if our Unification Church has faced much persecution here. Of course, the Daegu Church is engaged in various activities, but I hear that it has not yet become the central Unification Church in the country, and I thought that in the future, the people living in Gyeongbuk centered on Daegu must unite and advance together. I have said that we must advance and leap forward this year. Once again, we must advance and leap forward. Do you understand? "Yes." Do you promise? "Yes." Now, the content of 'Realizing the Kingdom of Heaven through Official Paths' is something I have not mentioned, but you all know it, and you have promised to do so.
So, the title or content I will speak about today is 'The Real World and the World of God's Will.' This is a big issue. Up until now, the world we live in does not fulfill God's will. It is a world that opposes the will, a world that destroys the will. This is what the Unification Church and general religions call 'the fallen world.'
What is the fallen world? It is a world that has nothing to do with God's will. Everything goes in the opposite direction. If God goes to the right, the current world goes to the left; if God goes forward, the current world goes backward. If God ascends, the current world descends. Because the current world is walking a path that is conflicting in every aspect, you must understand that the path from the current world to the world of God's will cannot be traversed without going through the opposite path.
Originally, a world without the fall is a world of peace, a world of unity. Furthermore, it is a world of love. There, God existed, the angelic world existed, and then the world of all creation existed, and the human world existed. Broadly speaking, there is a world centered on God, then the angelic world, and the created world centered on all creation, but even if we exclude this, the only beings that can interact with God personally are humans, so there exists the human world.
Therefore, God, angels, and humans could not be separated. They were always meant to be one. If they had become one, God would have been the subject, and humans would have become the object before the subject God, and the angelic world would have become a servant world that could serve both God and humans.
However, being a servant does not mean being lowly. Being a servant is not lowly, and being a master is not high. When connected in love, everything becomes one. To put it in human terms, it is like clothes, like a body, like a heart. God is like the heart, humans are like the body, and the angelic world is like the clothes.
If they had become one, it would have represented a universe of a completed personality. It would have become that world. That world would not have a conflict between upper and lower centered on principles, but upper and lower would correspond to each other, and the relative would harmonize with each other, and then front and back would correspond to each other. In that world, when the subject moves, the relative beings, regardless of what world or situation, would move according to the automatic principles, which is a world of order, a world of harmony, and a world of response.
From that perspective, it would be a world where everything is united centered on God's love. This is the principle. It is a world where God is trying to unfold the ideal of creation in the original world that has not fallen. This is how we see it.
That is why today, established church members or established church ministers often say, 'We must fulfill God's will.' However, when asked, 'What is God's will?' they become vague.
Once, I invited a famous theologian to our training session to speak in front of our young people, and he asked for questions. When he asked, 'Don't the students have any questions?' I asked, 'What is God's will?' The doctor replied, 'That is an easy yet difficult question.' What kind of easy yet difficult question is that? If it is easy, it is easy, and if it is difficult, it is difficult. That means he cannot say it clearly, and even if he does, it is not clear. (laughter)
To fulfill the will, one must first know what the will is
How can you fulfill something without knowing what it is? For any daily task, you must have a clear plan and discuss it, saying, 'We will definitely do it this way!' and then decide, 'Let's go!' Even if you make all these efforts, if you are vague about what the will is, you can never fulfill it. This is a theoretical conclusion. Therefore, as members of the Unification Church, to fulfill God's will, you must know the question, 'What is God's will?' Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
You said 'the world of will,' but what is God's will? "The Kingdom of Heaven on Earth…." What? That is too lofty. When asked, 'What is God's will?' you can answer, 'Since God is the Creator, He could not create without a purpose. Therefore, fulfilling the purpose of creation is God's will.' Isn't that right? In anything, if someone creates something, there is a purpose for that creation. Likewise, since the Creator God had a purpose, fulfilling that purpose is to fulfill God's will.
Then, what is the purpose of fulfilling God's purpose? Is it a purpose for the archangel, for God, or for humans? Since what is created is us humans, it must be a purpose for us humans. It is not a purpose for the archangel. It is a purpose for humans, so it is what humans must fulfill.
Then, what is the purpose that humans must fulfill? In the Garden of Eden, there were only Adam and Eve. One man and then? "A woman!" When you say 'woman,' if you reverse it, it becomes 'man.' When giving something, it is 'to give.' "Yes." There was one man and one woman. So, what is God's will for man and what is God's will for woman? There must be something. You all say, 'I live for God's will.' Women also say, 'I live for God's will,' and men say, 'I live for God's will.'
Then, what is God's will for man? It is to manifest as an objective being before God, with body and mind united. Why does it manifest as an objective being? Because by manifesting as an objective being, one can receive love from God on a personal level. Do you understand? The purpose lies in the matter of love. Ultimately, the destination is to enter the world of love.
We humans are structured dualistically. There is a mental existence and a physical existence, so the body and mind must become one. If the body and mind do not become one, everything will be divided. That is why people speak in double meanings. Everything is in double meanings and is chaotic. They keep talking about black words and white words, right?
Both the mind and body must be in the same posture. Thus, the body and mind must become one. If the body is completely good, the mind will also be completely good, and if the mind is completely good, the body will also be completely good. Therefore, when the subject and object, the internal and external, are completely united, the value of goodness will emerge. These are difficult words. Grandmothers may not understand well. Anyway, that is how it is.
If there is a man and a woman who want to stand in a position to fulfill God's will for individuals, how should it be? The body and mind must become one. Do you understand? To unite the body and mind…. Well, there are many people in the world whose body and mind are united, right? 'I am united in body and mind centered on our parents.' Such a person is called a filial child. Who are those parents? They are representatives of God. Today, in families, when parents are placed in the position of representatives of God, and in daily life, a person stands in a position to completely unite body and mind to love their parents, that person is undoubtedly called a filial child.
You talk about the way of loyalty and filial piety, but you do not know the definition. You must place parents in the family as the center like God, and by uniting body and mind, when the parents' love for their children does not change, a son or daughter who stands in a position to accept 100 percent and comply with that loving heart with body and mind is called a filial child! Today, you speak of the way of loyalty and filial piety, but you do not know the true way of loyalty and filial piety.
The true meaning of filial piety and loyalty
So, what is loyalty? Loyalty is nothing other than placing the king, who is the central figure of the nation, in the position of God's representative, and as God loves the nation, as long as that king, that sovereign, has a heart that loves the people, all citizens, whether male or female, regardless of rank or position, must unite and, as long as that love does not change, become citizens who say, 'We will love you with our whole body and mind in a relative position.' Such citizens are called loyal subjects! 
So, in this world, which is higher, a filial child or a loyal subject? Which is higher? "A loyal subject!" What is higher? "A loyal subject is higher." Is a filial child higher? "A loyal subject!" You must be clear about this. Is a filial child higher or a loyal subject? "A loyal subject!" A loyal subject is higher. You answered well.
To become a loyal subject, even if you must keep the duty of a filial child to your parents, if the nation is in crisis, if the country is facing a dire situation, in other words, if the North invades the South, then all citizens must rise up and establish the duty of loyalty for the nation.
In such a case, no matter how much a person is a filial child, they cannot say, 'I want to be a filial child. The nation has nothing to do with me. If the nation is to perish, let it perish. I can sacrifice my life for my parents with all my devotion and unity of body and mind, but the nation is irrelevant.' This is unacceptable.
However, even if one is in the position of a filial child, if they deny that and stand up for the nation with a heart that surpasses the love they had for their parents, can they love the nation's sovereign more than their parents? This is the issue. Do you understand? If you stand in a position that denies your parents and are in a position lower than loving your parents, that is not the path of loyalty. If you deny your parents, you must love the nation's sovereign with a heart that surpasses that of your parents, and a person who stands in a position of unity of body and mind towards that sovereign is undoubtedly a loyal subject. You must understand this. Do you understand? "Yes."
We must follow the path of the sage over the path of loyalty and filial piety
In our Republic of Korea, the ideology of loyalty and filial piety is truly good. So, does the people of the Republic of Korea only need to be loyal to the Republic of Korea? This is the question. Japanese people are...
Is it enough to be loyal only to the Emperor of Japan? Is it enough for a German to be loyal to the German sovereign? Or is it enough for an American citizen to just fulfill their duty of loyalty to the President of the United States? No. You need to understand this. It does not work that way. Is there a way to deny loyalty that transcends the nation? What is that way? It is the way of the sage. Do you understand? “Yes.” What way? “The way of the sage!” The way of the sage, the path that the sages walk.

Then who is the sage? If one is born a citizen of the Republic of Korea, they do not say, “I was born a citizen of the Republic of Korea, so I will only serve the Republic of Korea.” Such a person can become a great person. They can be a great figure of the Republic of Korea. There are many great figures, right? “Ah, he is a great person.” They can be recognized as a great person, but they cannot be a sage.

What is the path of the sage? They must treat all people as one nation. Regardless of race, regardless of the level of cultural development, regardless of gender and age, they must treat all people of the world as one brotherhood. They are all people of one nation. Is that different? They are all people of one nation. That is how they see it. And they think, “My loyalty and all my devotion is to treat all people of the world as one nation, and although there are many kings in the world, I will step over those kings and honor God, the King of all kings, and for that, I will transcend the path of filial piety and even sacrifice the path of loyalty.” What do we call such people? “Sages.” They are sages.

When I ask the citizens of the Republic of Korea, “Will you become sages, will you become loyal subjects?” and they respond, “The Republic of Korea is currently centered on loyalty and filial piety, so I do not know about sages. I will become a loyal subject.” This cannot be. Regardless of who it is, the path of loyalty is precious, but if there are new citizens who say they will walk the path of the sage, then those citizens will be able to bring blessings to the world before humanity!

What is a loyal subject? A loyal subject brings blessings to their nation before all the people of the world! Is that right? What is a filial child? A filial child brings blessings to their family! You need to understand that. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” What does a filial child do? “Brings blessings to the family….” A person who brings blessings to the family, and what about a loyal subject? “Brings blessings to the nation….” A person who brings blessings to the nation, and what about a sage? “Brings blessings to the world….” A person who brings blessings to the world.

So which path will you choose among these? “The path of the sage.” If a high school teacher were here, they might say, “Mr. Moon, you are wrong. I am the discipline head of a high school, and what you are saying today is incorrect.” No matter how much they say it is wrong, the person who says it is wrong is wrong, not me. It may seem like I am saying something incorrect, but I am not wrong. Do you understand?

So, who were the people that became the central ideologies of history and the objects of all admiration, leading to a brilliant cultural world beyond history? They were not those who died with the great name of loyal subjects for their nation, but those who brought the way of the sage before all humanity beyond history. This fact is proven by history. Do you understand?

Then who is God? God loves, but does not love within the boundaries of nations. If it is the Republic of Korea, He does not only love the people of the Republic of Korea, the yellow race, the people of the Korean Peninsula. He lifts all the people of the Republic of Korea and says, “These guys!” I apologize for saying that. (Laughter) He takes them by the neck and says, “Oh, you are not going to fall to the ground.” He asks, “Why aren’t you falling?” and lifts them up to the world. He wants them to live at the center of the world. If you can stand completely in such a position, you will be blessed. You will receive blessings from the world.

The reality of the world and the world of God's will
I am doing this because I know God better than anyone else.
If there were no God, it would be one thing, but if there is a God, who is the greatest king in the world? “God.” If there are pastors here, they might feel uncomfortable, but God is the greatest king. In the world of power, He is the greatest king, right? Isn’t that so? This needs to be said to feel the reality of it. He must be called the greatest king…. (Laughter) Now, in this universe, if there is a great king, who is it? “God.” Only the followers of the Unification Church who believe in God would say that; do others know whether God exists or not? Have you seen God? Have you touched God? Have you even sucked on God's finger? Is it salty? Is it refreshing? (Laughter) If you ask like this, it becomes difficult. You can answer like this: God exists in formlessness….

Let me tell you one thing. Today, communists and so-called intellectuals, especially world-renowned scholars, boastfully say, “Where is God? That is all made up by the weak.” Communists say that. They also say, “Lower animals evolved into humans!” but that is all nonsense. That is not true. I have studied in that area, but they speak without knowing. It turns out that God clearly exists.

If there were no God, this Reverend Moon would not have become so famous today. If there were no God, I would not have been insulted. If there were no God, I would have lived in a rural hut in North Pyongan Province, living in the same position as your grandfathers, becoming a father and mother, giving birth to sons and daughters, and thinking, “Oh, my sons and daughters must live well.” I would have lived like that. There would be no need to cause a stir in the world, to cause a stir in the Republic of Korea, to live as a problematic figure, as a problematic man everywhere. But does that mean I have gained anything? Have I gained money? What is food? I have lost all my food to eat and all my money to use.

Why do I do this? Because I know God better than anyone else…. Because I know what God loves the most, I do this work. To explain that would take too long, so I will say there is no God! Unification Church members, there is no God! There is no God! “There is!” (Laughter) There is not! “There is!” Oh…. (Laughter) I want to curse. There is no God! “There is!” There is not! “There is!” Thank you for answering that there is. Since you say there is, I will also say there is. There is! When someone says there is not, and you say there is, it is easy, isn’t it? That is why I say it. God exists!

God is the subject who governs the whole
Then who is God? He is the subject who governs all. He is the absolute subject. There is a saying, “Human hearts change morning and evening, but the colors of the mountains remain the same through the ages,” but that subject is not one who changes morning and evening. Once He says, “It is good,” even if you go to the bottom of a black hell and ask, “How about God?” He will say, “It is good.” Even if you ask, “Is it good here even though it is dark?” He will still say, “It is good.” He will say, “It is good” even when you go to a bright place. Once He has said He is good, that is eternal. Once He starts to love, He does not give up halfway; He loves forever. This is absolute truth. It is truly wonderful.

Knowing such things, I do this work. I am a smart person. Now, the Korean people will think well of me. Pastors who oppose the Unification Church will gather together and say, “What about Mr. Moon? He dances naked….” (Laughter) They make up all sorts of things, but if someone hears that and asks, “Hey, do you know that well? Yes, Mr. Moon is not good. He is not as good as you!” they will be surprised. “Well, if you compare the opposing pastor and Mr. Moon, who is better?” they will have to say, “Mr. Moon is better.” (Laughter) That is how it has become. Do you understand?

For 30 years, they have been saying I am bad, bad, bad from the pulpit every day, and as time has passed, the result is that those who have been cursing have been recognized as fools, and those who were cursed have risen like God. Isn’t that so? If you were to go to a principal of a middle or high school and ask, “Principal! Who is higher, you or Mr. Moon?” they would say, “Mr. Moon is higher!” (Laughter) Korea has come this far.

At this point, I can boast more than anyone else, and I have more spirit than anyone else, and I do everything with determination. This Mr. Moon…. Because I know God, I do this work. So, what is God? “The Absolute Being!”

When it is time to answer, you should say “Yes” immediately when asked, but why don’t you? This is the worst habit of Koreans. “You rascal!” Only then do they say “Yes, yes.” (Laughter) What is there? You people from Daegu, Gyeongsang Province! Don’t laugh for no reason. Later, if I throw insults at your laughing faces, you might go “Hmm.” What do you call people from Gyeongsang Province? “Mokgoti!” Do they listen to others or not? I am not resembling a person from Gyeongsang Province; a person from Gyeongsang Province resembles me. (Laughter)

God is the highest being. Do you understand? Therefore, to truly be a filial child who can be loved by Him, one must transcend the nation. Those who cannot do that cannot be loved by God as filial children. Those who cannot transcend the family also cannot….

One must transcend the family, ride the history of loyalty, and then follow the way of the sage, so that all the people of the world can praise, “Ah, he is a wonderful person,” and can look up and praise, “That person must surely be a child of God.” Without reaching that position, is there a qualification to be a child of the absolute being of the universe? Is there or not? “There is not!” Surely? “There is not!”

To love the whole world, heaven and earth
Now, when God looks, does He want to love all of Asia, or does He want to love only the Republic of Korea? “All of Asia….” Is that certain? “Yes.” Then are you all not Koreans who have learned the spirit of loyalty and filial piety? 
When God looks, does He want to love the world, or does He want to love Asia? “The world.” Koreans call Japanese, Chinese, all sorts of names. They call Americans, Soviets, British, all kinds of names, and there is nothing that is not derogatory. (Laughter) But can they be loved? “No.” Where did this ideology come from…. When I look closely, these are foolish people who have been rolling around for 5,000 years without being able to take off their foolish hats, and they have no place to rest their backs. They just keep rolling around…. What should I say? Surume, Surume is a Japanese word, but what? “Squid!” (Laughter) They have become flat like dried squid, and what of it…. But their eyes seem to be open, right? (Laughter) They call everyone a “guy.” What guy, what guy…. They don’t even call them people. They don’t call them gentlemen either.

When God sees that, God wants to love and live with the world, but when He sees people from the Republic of Korea saying, “Those bastards, those things!” would God feel good? “No.” He thinks, “They must have studied a lot about what kind of guy they are because they couldn’t live for 5,000 years.” What guy, what guy….

In the past, they used to say “lowly person, gentleman,” but gentlemen do not have the character “guy.” That has risen. (Laughter)

When I see this, God…. So, they couldn’t live for 5,000 years. It may not be solely because of that, but there is something that can be said. If a neighbor or someone in the neighborhood is doing well…. If a cousin buys a field, they feel envious? “If they buy a field!” Why? Because they are doing better than them….

When God looks, He thinks that loving the world beyond Asia is better than just loving Asia. Furthermore, going one step further, since God is a spiritual being, when He looks, He does not only look at the humans living on this planet of 4 billion people. He also looks at the countless spirits who have come to this earth over thousands of years and have gone to the spirit world, whether they are in hell or in the intermediate spirit world.

Therefore, when God looks, if someone says, “Let’s only love all humanity and the people on this earth,” God might think, “That is possible.” However, if there are those who say, “Let’s love not only the earth but also the spirit world and the physical world,” what will God do? He will stroke His beard and say, “You guys, love well.” (Laughter) Isn’t that so? “Yes.” Isn’t that right? “Yes.”

No matter how much one says they love the world and heaven and earth, in the end, it is not that they say, “I only love the world and heaven and earth, but I dislike God.” Rather, when they say, “Loving the whole world like this is for the purpose of loving you,” God will be happier. He will stroke His beard and laugh, “Hahaha!” (Laughter)

The way to get a perfect score even without knowing the formula
Now, looking at it this way, there are many formulas, but if you skip them and just get the answers right on the test, God will give you a perfect score. Isn’t that good? (Laughter) When taking a test, if you solve the formulas all mixed up, that is all fine, but if you just get the answer right, you get a perfect score. Isn’t that simple? But what is the answer? It is to love God only. Then you will get a perfect score on all tests. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”

God, who wants to love humanity in such a way, has come to this conclusion after much patience. How wonderful is that? God was waiting for that, thinking that the world would compete, but the people of the world have fallen out and do not even dream of it. That is why God had no choice but to think, “If you love only God absolutely, what will the score be on all tests?” “Perfect score!” Regardless of the formula, all? “Perfect score!” Perfect score! (Laughter) It is a perfect score. So, He is a grateful being, isn’t He? “He is a grateful being.”

In any religion, if one delves into the deep world of that religion, of course, the doctrines of that religion are necessary, and there are many stories, but beyond those doctrines and stories, what is more necessary is to love the God who is the center of this universe, who is absolute. Then everything will pass. Everything will be passed.

That grandmother and grandfather have passed away, right? Ah, they must have gone deaf, I apologize. (Laughter) I came to see the faces of grandmothers in Daegu after a long time, but they are deaf…. The world cannot be helped. As time goes by, all signs of the above will occur. Now that they are old and deaf, they should not listen to external sounds but should listen to internal sounds. And they should prepare to go to a good place. When you understand that God created life, it is truly interesting.

When you get old, you become deaf and blind, right? You become blind, deaf, and even lose your sense of smell. What does this mean? It is to make you aware of internal flavors. Therefore, to become a complete person, to become an ideal person, to develop spiritual tastes and senses, that is why it happens. Therefore, becoming deaf is a blessing, isn’t it? Is it not? Is it bad or good? “It is good.” (Laughter) Is becoming blind good or bad? “It is good.” (Laughter)

If you think this way, you can lament your own unhappy self in the present reality.
There are grandmothers and grandfathers who can hum a tune and express gratitude before God. This ideology is frightening. When the perspective of what one sees and feels is different, everything is turned upside down. The opposite world is not a miserable one, but rather an amazing world that we can digest as happiness. We need to understand that.

So, if one were to score a perfect hundred in everything and go to God, would that God say He doesn't know? Would He say He knows? Among fallen humans, there is no one who can be recognized by God as having scored a hundred. No matter how great a pastor, doctor, or any great saint may be, when God looks at them, there is no one who can be acknowledged as having scored a hundred.

Thus, humanity is astonishing. Is this valuable or not? "It is not valuable." We need to recognize that. Established church pastors say, "What about this person or that person from the Unification Church...," but we should disregard all that. Do they have the qualification to say that to me? Go see in the spirit world. They are the lowest of the low, and they are all people who cannot even go to heaven. Do you think I am doing this because I am worse than them? No matter how you look at it, whether in terms of strength, ability, or skill, I surpass them... That's right. (Laughter) Those who are new here, I am saying this. If anyone feels uncomfortable, they can feel uncomfortable. If it hurts, they should either die or hang on and see. They cannot just live or die for a thousand years. That won't do. We must see it through to the end.

When God looks, there is no one who can score a perfect hundred.

Now, our ladies, are there no beauties among our Unification Church members here in Daegu? The men are handsome, but the women... They look like they have opened up like a gourd in a roof tile. (Laughter) Especially the women from Gyeongsangdo, they look fierce. Their cheekbones stick out, and they are full of greed. That might make you feel uncomfortable. I say this to make you feel uncomfortable. Yes, even if it feels uncomfortable, you should at least feel the impression. If you just sit at home, you won't encounter such uncomfortable things, but if you go see Mr. Moon today and feel uncomfortable, that discomfort could be a blessing. Do you understand? Gyeongsangdo women, I mean. (Laughter)

Why do they have big faces, like lion faces? Being in the Western world, I feel that even though they are short, their faces are all big. (Laughter) So, I thought positively, "Oh, they must be deep thinkers." Why did they live so hard? If one is dull, they can only do labor, so they work hard to earn money, thinking that they will eventually lose it all. They thought they would lose everything to the communists. Isn't that right?
